| **5** | [InboxDollars](https://www.inboxdollars.com) | Rewards platform offering cash for surveys, games, and online activities [(💰 pricing)](https://www.inboxdollars.com/rewards) [(🚀 quick start)](https://www.inboxdollars.com/register) | Free to join and participate | <br>• Cash rewards instead of points<br>• Multiple earning options<br>• Signup bonus<br>• Daily surveys and games | Complete surveys, play games, watch videos, read emails, and shop online | ⭐⭐⭐ (3/5) |
